Get the DM authorization for user to use best effort IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is disabled. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access only (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL). \\
\hline
{\em 2} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+TE access. \\
\hline
{\em 3} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+T\+E/\+H\+S\+PA access. \\
\hline
{\em 4} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for A\+NY access except 2G access.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_db_a2bfc2be39e10f52df6157d0b95c5e7bc}{Mtc\+Call\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Db\+Set\+Dm\+Rcs\+Ip\+Video\+Call\+Auth}}

Get the DM authorization for user to use best effort IP Voice Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & Indicates that best effort IP Voice Call service is disabled. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indicates that best effort IP Voice Call service is enabled for non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access only (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL). \\
\hline
{\em 2} & Indicates that best effort IP Voice Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+TE access. \\
\hline
{\em 3} & Indicates that best effort IP Voice Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+T\+E/\+H\+S\+PA access. \\
\hline
{\em 4} & Indicates that best effort IP Voice Call service is enabled for A\+NY access except 2G access.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static boolean com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Db\+Get\+Ip\+Call\+Break\+Out (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Get a device in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode whether it can initiate Voice calls even if the recipient user does not show service capability for voice calls. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode. It will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the best effort IP Voice Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em true} & Indicates an IP Voice Call cannot be initiated if an error (480/404) is returned to a request for the recipient user\textquotesingle{}s service capabilities or service capabilities do not indicate the support of IP Voice Call. \\
\hline
{\em false} & Indicates an IP Voice Call to be initiated even if an error (480/404) is returned to a request for the recipient user?s service capabilities or service capabilities do not indicate the support of IP Voice Call.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Get privacy option from database. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em uc\+Opt} & Privacy option type, it can be one of M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE, M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+ID, M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER, M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+I\+ON and M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+V\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em true} & Corresponding privacy option is enable. \\
\hline
{\em false} & Corresponding privacy option is disable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

Get the Ue authorization for user to use best effort IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is disabled. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access only (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL). \\
\hline
{\em 2} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+TE access. \\
\hline
{\em 3} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+T\+E/\+H\+S\+PA access. \\
\hline
{\em 4} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for A\+NY access except 2G access.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

Get an R\+C\+S-\/\+CS device whether it can initiate a best effort IP Video Call upgrade without first tearing down the CS voice call. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+CS mode. It is will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em true} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can be initiated even before the CS voice call is torn down. \\
\hline
{\em false} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can only be initiated once the CS voice call has been torn down.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static boolean com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Db\+Get\+V\+Call\+Upg\+On\+Cap\+Error (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Get an R\+C\+S-\/\+AA or R\+C\+S-\/\+CS device whether it can initiate a best effort IP Video Call upgrade even if service capability exchange fails with 480 Temporarily Unavailable or 408 Timeout. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode or in R\+C\+S-\/\+CS mode. It is will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em true} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can be initiated even if 480/408 error is returned. \\
\hline
{\em false} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can only be initiated if the capability is returned from the request for the recipient user\textquotesingle{}s service capabilities.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Set a device in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode whether it can initiate Voice calls even if the recipient user does not show service capability for voice calls. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode. It will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the best effort IP Voice Call service.

\end{DoxyParams}

Set a device in R\+C\+S-\/\+CS mode whether it can initiate Voice calls even if the recipient user does not show service capability for voice calls. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+CS mode. It will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the best effort IP Voice Call service.
